The website's critical consensus reads, "''Baywatch'' takes its source material's [[Jiggle television|jiggle factor]] to R-rated levels, but lacks the original's campy charm – and leaves its charming stars flailing in the shallows."<ref>{{cite web|title=Baywatch (2017)|url=https://www.rottentomatoes.com/m/baywatch_2017|access-date=October 26, 2020|work=[[Rotten Tomatoes]]|publisher=[[Fandango Media]]}}</ref>

TITLE Paddington 2

OLD It received widespread critical acclaim on [[Metacritic]], and had an [[List of films with a 100% rating on Rotten Tomatoes|approval rating of 100%]] on [[Rotten Tomatoes]] (and was, with 245 positive reviews, the highest-rated film on the site until a negative review was registered at 246).

NEW It received widespread critical acclaim on [[Metacritic]], and had an [[List of films with a 99% rating on Rotten Tomatoes|approval rating of 99%]] on [[Rotten Tomatoes]] (and was, with 245 positive reviews, the highest-rated film on the site until a negative review was registered at 246).<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.rottentomatoes.com/m/paddington_2|title=Paddington 2|website=[[Rotten Tomatoes]]|publisher=[[Fandango Media]]|access-date=August 28, 2021}}</ref>

FLAGS {'missing count', 'missing average', 'WL:Metacritic', 'no longer 0% or 100%', 'Metacritic'}

OLD On review aggregator [[Rotten Tomatoes]], ''Paddington 2'' has an approval rating of 99% based on 246 reviews, with an average rating of 8.7/10.
